+/******************************************************************************
+ * \\brief Name:        DemExt_ClearDTC
+ * \
     Description: Requesting the UDS ClearDiagnosticInformation (0x14) service from the DEM
+ *
+ *                     This function handling the UDS ClearDiagnosticInformation
+ *                     (0x14) service request communication between the DCM and the DEM.
+ * \\param [in] DTC: DTC ID
+ * \\param [in] DTCFormat: Format of DTC, OBD or UDS
+ * \\param [in] DTCOrigin: Memory origin of the DTC
+ *****************************************************************************/
+Std_ReturnType DemExt_ClearDTC (uint32 DTC, Dem_DTCFormatType DTCFormat, Dem_DTCOriginType DTCOrigin)/* PRQA S 3206 */
+{
+
+  Std_ReturnType retStatus = E_OK;
+
+  /* Lock the fault reporting */
+  BswErrDeb_SetFltReportLockClrDtc();
+
+  /* Forwarding request to DEM */
+  //retStatus = Rte_Call_DemExt_Dcm_ClearDTC(DTC, DTCFormat, DTCOrigin);
+
+
+    /* Initiate fault reset */
+    BswErrDeb_ReqClrDtcFltRst();
+    /* clears the reset counter and writes the value to NvM */
+    RstHndlr_ClrRstCntr();
+  
+
+  return retStatus;
+}

+/******************************************************************************
+ * \\brief   Name:           Rsh_CalPLKIniPosn_Start
+ * \
       Description:    Start function for Park lock Routine 0x0120,
+ * \\param   [in]  OpStatus : operation status ()
+ * \\param   [out] routinestatus : out data 
+ * \\param   [out] ErrorCode: NRC
+ * \\return  Success of operation.
+ * \\retval  E_OK
+ * \\work item ID: 100kW-42970
+ *****************************************************************************/
+FUNC(Std_ReturnType, RSH_CODE) Rsh_CalPLKIniPosn_Start(Dcm_OpStatusType OpStatus, P2VAR(uint8, AUTOMATIC, RTE_RSH_APPL_VAR) routinestatus, P2VAR(Dcm_NegativeResponseCodeType, AUTOMATIC, RTE_RSH_APPL_VAR) ErrorCode)/* PRQA S 3432,3206 */
+{
+   Std_ReturnType status_CalPLKIniPosnStart = E_OK;
+
+   if(NULL_PTR != routinestatus)
+   {
+      /*! \\misra Msg(4:3112): This statement has no side-effect - it can be removed.
+       * The statement is an ASR conform suppression of an input parameter */
+      TS_PARAM_UNUSED(OpStatus); /*PRQA S 3112*/
+      if(FALSE == BswC2cData.ParkLockMgrCalibTestEna)
+      {
+         /* Set Parklock calibration test request */
+         BswC2cData.ParkLockMgrCalibTestEna = TRUE;
+         /* routine Lunched */ 
+         *routinestatus = 0x00u;
+      }
+      else
+      {
+         /* routine already started */
+         *routinestatus = 0x02u;
+      }
+   } 
+   return status_CalPLKIniPosnStart;
+}
+
+/******************************************************************************
+ * \\brief   Name:           Rsh_CalPLKIniPosn_RequestResults
+ * \
       Description:    RequestResults function for Park lock Routine 0x0120,
+ * \\param   [in]  OpStatus : operation status ()
+ * \\param   [out] RequestResOutSignal : out data 
+ * \\param   [out] ErrorCode: NRC
+ * \\return  Success of operation.
+ * \\retval  E_OK
+ * \\work item ID: 100kW-42970
+ *****************************************************************************/
+FUNC(Std_ReturnType, RSH_CODE) Rsh_CalPLKIniPosn_RequestResults(Dcm_OpStatusType OpStatus, P2VAR(uint8, AUTOMATIC, RTE_RSH_APPL_VAR) RequestResOutSignal, P2VAR(Dcm_NegativeResponseCodeType, AUTOMATIC, RTE_RSH_APPL_VAR) ErrorCode)/* PRQA S 3432,3206 */
+{
+   Std_ReturnType status_CheckProgCondRequestResults = E_OK;
+
+   if(NULL_PTR != RequestResOutSignal)
+   {
+      /*! \\misra Msg(4:3112): This statement has no side-effect - it can be removed.
+       * The statement is an ASR conform suppression of an input parameter */
+      TS_PARAM_UNUSED(OpStatus); /*PRQA S 3112*/
+      if( E_OK == SftyC2cData.CalibTestRngVld)
+      { 
+         /* Routine completed successfully */
+         *RequestResOutSignal = 0x01u;
+      }
+      else
+      {
+         /* Calibration error */
+         *RequestResOutSignal = 0x02u;
+      }
+      /* reset Parklock calibration test request */
+      BswC2cData.ParkLockMgrCalibTestEna = FALSE;
+   } 
+   return status_CheckProgCondRequestResults;
+}
